The bathroom and shower room are independent, and there is a special dressing table. There is a large cloakroom, and the room is very clean! They took the initiative to prepare bathtub covers and disposable toilet seats, which is really considerate! 
The room delivers 4 kinds of fruits every day, and there are 6 kinds of drinks in the refrigerator, as well as potato chips and cookies. The cookies are very delicious and replenished every day. The room is equipped with Lily's coffee capsule machine, and 3 cans of Yakult are prepared for the children every day. Mineral water is not enough for 6 bottles every day, which is very generous! 
The room prepares 4 kinds of tea every day. The highlight is that the teapot and teacup are wrapped in plastic wrap, which is very clean and reliable! 
Service: The attitude of the front desk, cleaning, and concierge is very good. I saw that there were children who took the initiative to prepare children's pillows. The room is cleaned very clean every day! 
Facilities: There is a book bar and a gym, and almost no one goes there. It is very quiet and the book bar is well decorated. 
Breakfast has everything you should have, noodles, wontons, porridge, fried eggs, steamed snacks, cold dishes, bread and pastries, and coffee machines. The feature is that there are 4 kinds of freshly squeezed juice every day! This is not available in many hotels, and it is especially friendly to children! A takeaway cup is also provided, so you can pack your own juice to take away. You can drink Yakult for breakfast. There are also 4-5 kinds of pre-brewed teas prepared for breakfast every day, which is also very considerate to the elderly! It is really not an exaggeration to say that it feels like home!
